////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Tadb_Trv.txt : Complement to Tadb.txt containing
//						radiator valve and thermostatic head
//						definitions
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
// For thermostatic heads and radiator valves.
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CTable(TRVTYPE_TAB) -> LIST_TAB
{
	"Thermostatic valve types"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

new:CTable(TRVALV_TAB) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
	"Thermostatic valves"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

new:CTable(RVACCESSOR_TAB) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
	"Return valve accessories"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

new:CTable(FLCTRLVALV_TAB) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
	"Flow limited control valves"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

new:CTable(FLCV_CHAR_TAB) -> MISC_TAB
{
	"Flow limited control valve characteristics"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

new:CTableSet(TRVHEADSET_TAB) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
	"Thermostatic valve/Head sets"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table TRVTYPE_TAB : ordered enumeration of the types of
//							thermostatic valves
//
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
// !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
// The incremented numbers for TRVTYPE_TAB must take into account
// the max number in CVTYPE_TAB (To get correct priority in
// DialogTechParam/CV/Hydro circ preferences).
// !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_StringID(TRVTYPE_PRESET)->TRVTYPE_TAB
{
	{
		"IDS_TRVTYPE_PRESET"
	}
	10
	TRVALV_TAB
}

new:CDB_StringID(TRVTYPE_NOPRSET)->TRVTYPE_TAB
{
	{
		"IDS_TRVTYPE_NOPRSET"
	}
	11
	TRVALV_TAB
}

new:CDB_StringID(TRVTYPE_FLOWLIMITED)->TRVTYPE_TAB
{
	{
		"IDS_TRVTYPE_FLOWLIMITED"
	}
	12
	FLCTRLVALV_TAB
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table CTRL_PROP_TAB : Table of control properties
//
//	new:CDB_ControlProperties(ID\1) -> CTRL_PROP_TAB
//	{
//		CV 2W3W enum
//		CV Func enum
//		Control characteristic enum
//		Mixing/Dividing enum
//		PushClose enum
//		BCVType enum
//	}
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_ControlProperties(CP_TRV) -> CTRL_PROP_TAB
{
	#eCV2W3W_CV2W							// Number of ports of the control valve. Can be #eCV2W3W_CVNU, eCV2W3W_CV2W, eCV2W3W_CV3W or eCV2W3W_CV4W.
	#eCVFUNC_Presettable                    // Control valve type. Can be #eCVFUNC_NoControl, #eCVFUNC_ControlOnly, #eCVFUNC_Presettable, #eCVFUNC_PresetPT or #eCVFUNC_Electronic.
	#eCTRLCHAR_NotChar                      // Control characteristic. Can be #eCTRLCHAR_NotChar, #eCTRLCHAR_Linear or #eCTRLCHAR_EqualPc.
	#eMIXDIV_None                           // Mixing or dividing mode. Can be #eMIXDIV_None, #eMIXDIV_Mixing or #eMIXDIV_Dividing.
	#ePUSHCLOSE_True                        // Push or pull to close. Can be #ePUSHCLOSE_Undef, #ePUSHCLOSE_False or #ePUSHCLOSE_True.
	#eBcvType_None                          // BCV type. Can be #eBcvType_None, #eBcvType_KvSeries, #eBcvType_LiftLimit, #eBcvType_CharIndep or #eBcvType_Electronic.
}

new:CDB_ControlProperties(CP_RVT) -> CTRL_PROP_TAB
{
	#eCV2W3W_CV2W							// Number of ports of the control valve. Can be #eCV2W3W_CVNU, eCV2W3W_CV2W, eCV2W3W_CV3W or eCV2W3W_CV4W.
	#eCVFUNC_ControlOnly                    // Control valve type. Can be #eCVFUNC_NoControl, #eCVFUNC_ControlOnly, #eCVFUNC_Presettable, #eCVFUNC_PresetPT or #eCVFUNC_Electronic.
	#eCTRLCHAR_NotChar                      // Control characteristic. Can be #eCTRLCHAR_NotChar, #eCTRLCHAR_Linear or #eCTRLCHAR_EqualPc.
	#eMIXDIV_None                           // Mixing or dividing mode. Can be #eMIXDIV_None, #eMIXDIV_Mixing or #eMIXDIV_Dividing.
	#ePUSHCLOSE_True                        // Push or pull to close. Can be #ePUSHCLOSE_Undef, #ePUSHCLOSE_False or #ePUSHCLOSE_True.
	#eBcvType_None                          // BCV type. Can be #eBcvType_None, #eBcvType_KvSeries, #eBcvType_LiftLimit, #eBcvType_CharIndep or #eBcvType_Electronic.
}


////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table VALVE_CHAR_TAB : Table of valve characteristics
//
//	new:CDB_ValveCharacteristic(ID\1) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			Discrete/Continuous: 				#eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
//			Single/Multi/Electronic-turn: 		#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
//			SettingRounding						Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
//		}
//		Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
//		Min recommended setting (for selection)
//		Number of curves
//		opening 1 \ Kv 1
//		opening 2 \ Kv 2
//		...
//	}
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_ValveCharacteristic(C_REGULUX) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
{
	{
		#eDISCRETE_False						// #eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
		#eTURN_Multi                            // #eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
		0.5										// Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
	}
	0.0                                     // Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
	1.0                                     // Min recommended setting (for selection)
	1                                       // Number of curves
	0.00 \ 0.09                             // opening 1 \ Kv 1
	0.50 \ 0.19
	1.00 \ 0.30
	2.00 \ 0.65
	3.00 \ 1.01
	4.00 \ 1.31
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table VALVE_CHAR_TAB : Table of valve characteristics
//
//	new:CDB_ThermoCharacteristic(ID\1) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				Discrete/Continuous: 				#eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
//				Single/Multi/Electronic-turn: 		#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
//				SettingRounding						Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
//			}
//			Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
//			Min recommended setting (for selection)
//			Number of curves
//			Opening 1 \ Kv catalogue [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
//			Opening 2 \ Kv catalogue [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
//			...
//		}
//		Opening 1 \ Kv 1K \ Kv 2K \ ...
//		Opening 2 \ Kv 1k \ Kv 2K \ ...
//		...
//	}
//
// Remark: it's possible to introduce a curve at 2K without 1K. In this case we have to write:
//			  Opening 1 \ -1.0 \ Kv1
//			  Opening 2 \ -1.0 \ Kv2
//            ...
//         and fill the first curve will all the values to -1.0.
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_ThermoCharacteristic(C_CALYPSOTRV3) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
{
	{
		{
			#eDISCRETE_False						// #eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
			#eTURN_Single                           // #eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
			0.5										// Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
		}
		0.0                                     // Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
		1.0                                     // Min recommended setting (for selection)
		1                                       // Number of curves
		0.00 \ 0.000                            // opening 1 \ Kv 1
		1.00 \ 0.010
		2.00 \ 0.038
		3.00 \ 0.073
		4.00 \ 0.092
		5.00 \ 0.142
		6.00 \ 0.261
		7.00 \ 0.398
		8.00 \ 0.544
	}
	0.00 \ 0.000 \ 0.000                    // Opening 1 \ Kv 1K \ Kv 2K \ ...
	1.00 \ 0.010 \ 0.010
	2.00 \ 0.038 \ 0.038
	3.00 \ 0.073 \ 0.073
	4.00 \ 0.087 \ 0.092
	5.00 \ 0.120 \ 0.142
	6.00 \ 0.225 \ 0.259
	7.00 \ 0.304 \ 0.389
	8.00 \ 0.361 \ 0.520
}

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//								CDB_FLCVCharacteristic
//
//	CDB_FLCVCharacteristic is for the flow limited control valve.
//
//	new:CDB_FLCVCharacteristic(ID\1) -> FLCV_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			Discrete/Continuous: 				eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
//			Single/Multi/Electronic-turn: 		#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
//			SettingRounding						Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
//		}
//		Dpmax						Max differential pressure (60KPa).
//		DpminLF						Min differential pressure at low flow (10KPa).
//      QLFmin						Flow min for 'DpminLF' (10l/h).
//      QLFmax						Flow max for 'DpminLF' (100l/h).
//		DpminNF						Min differential pressure at normal flow (15KPa)
//      QNFmin						Flow min for 'DpminNF' (100l/h).
//      QNFmax						Flow max for 'DpminNF' (150l/h).
//		Setting 1 \ Flow 1
//		Setting 2 \ Flow 2
//		...
//	}
//
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table TRVALV_TAB : Thermostatic radiator valves
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	How to write a thermostatic valve information ?
//	-----------------------------------------------
//
//	new:CDB_ThermostaticValve(ID)->tableID	Common CData syntax
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						{
//							{
//								0				isDeleted
//								1				isAvailable
//								0				isHidden
//								1				isFix
//								0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//								0				Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
//      						0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//							}
//							Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//							PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//							Tmax in �C
//							Tmin in �C
//						}
//						"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//						"Name"					Name of the product
//						TypeID					Identifier of the valve type
//						FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//						VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//						PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//						Comment					Product comment
//						ProdImgID				Product image ID
//						AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//						PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
//						TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//						Price					Price of the product
// 						ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//						AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//						isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   					AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//						AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//					}
//					BodyMaterialID			Identifier of the body material
//					SizeID					Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//					ConnectID				Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//					ConnTabID				Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//					Conn2ID					Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//					CBIType					Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//					CBISize					Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//					CBISizeInch				Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//					CBICompatibilityIndex	CBI compatibility Index
//					CBIVersion				CBI Version
//					Dpmax					Maximum Dp of the valve
//					MeasPt					Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
//					MeasurableData			Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
//					InletSizeID				Identifier of the inlet size ID
//					OutletSizeID			Identifier of the outlet size ID
//				}
//				CharactID			// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in ThermoCharID
//			}
//			Kvs					Kvs of the CV
//			Stroke				Stroke of the CV
//			Rangeability		Rangeability of the CV
//			LeakageRate			Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
//			CloseOffCharID		Identifier of the close-off characteristic
//			ActuatorGroupID		Identifier of the actuator group
//			CvAdapterGroupID	Identifier of the CV adapter group
//			CtrlPropID			Identifier of the control properties
//			AdapterListMode		Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
//								(see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
//		}
//		ThermoCharID		Identifier of the thermostatic characteristic
//		"Description"		Description of the product
//	}
//
// Inherited files
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_TAProduct::BodyMaterialID
//	CDB_TAProduct::SizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnectID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnTabID
//	CDB_TAProduct::Conn2ID
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIType
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISize
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISizeInch
//  CDB_TAProduct::CBICompatibilityIndex
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIVersion
//	CDB_TAProduct::Dpmax
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasPt
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasurableData
//	CDB_TAProduct::InletSizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::OutletSizeID
//	CDB_RegulatingValve::CharactID
//	CDB_ControlValve::Kvs
//	CDB_ControlValve::Stroke
//	CDB_ControlValve::Rangeability
//	CDB_ControlValve::LeakageRate
//	CDB_ControlValve::CloseOffCharID
//	CDB_ControlValve::ActuatorGroupID
//	CDB_ControlValve::CvAdapterGroupID
//	CDB_ControlValve::CtrlPropID
//	CDB_ControlValve::AdapterListMode
//	CDB_ThermostaticValve::ThermoCharID
//	CDB_ThermostaticValve::Description
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


//****************************
// Presettable
//****************************

/////////////////
// Straight
/////////////////

new:CDB_ThermostaticValve(CALYPSOTRV3_10D_TRV) -> TRVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					{
						{
							0													// isDeleted
							1                                                   // isAvailable
							0                                                   // isHidden
							1                                                   // isFix
							0                                                   // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
							0                                                   // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
							0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
						}
						0.6e+6 \ 1.0e+6   									// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
						NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
						120.0                                               // Tmax in �C
						-10.0                                               // Tmin in �C
					}
					"50 820-010"  										// Reference to the TA Product
					"Calypso TRV-3 10"                                  // Name of the product
					TRVTYPE_PRESET                                      // Identifier of the valve type
					FAM_CALYPSOTRV3                                     // Identifier of the family of the product
					VERS_STRAIGHT                                       // Identifier of the version of the product
					1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
					""                                                  // Product comment
					"TA_TRV"                                            // Product image ID
					ACCGR_RADCON_10                                     // Identifier of the accessory group
					#ePartOfaSetNo                                      // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
					NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
					0.0                                                 // Price of the product
					#eProduct                              	            // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
					NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
					0                                                   // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
					NO_ID                                      	        // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
					NO_ID										        // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth
				}
				BDY_BRASS 											// Identifier of the body material
				DN_10                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
				CONN_METRIC_THR                                     // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
				""                                                  // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
				0                                                   // CBI compatibility Index
				""                                                  // CBI Version
				3.0e+4                                              // Maximum Dp of the valve
				#eMeasPointNone                                     // Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
				#eMeasDataNone                                      // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
				NO_ID											// Identifier of the inlet size ID
				NO_ID											// Identifier of the outlet size ID
			}
			NO_ID                                    			// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in ThermoCharID
		}
		0.80												// Kvs of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Stroke of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Rangeability of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
		ACTGR_HEIM_TRV                                      // Identifier of the actuator group
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the CV adapter group
		CP_TRV                                              // Identifier of the control properties
		#eCVAdapterListNA									// Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                            // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
	}
	C_CALYPSOTRV3											// Identifier of the thermostatic characteristic
	""					                                // Description of the product
}

new:CDB_ThermostaticValve(CALYPSOTRV3_15D_TRV) -> TRVALV_TAB
{ Inherited(CALYPSOTRV3_10D_TRV)
	{
		CDB_Product::Reference	= "50 820-015"
		CDB_Product::Name		= "Calypso TRV-3 15"
		CDB_Product::AccessGroupID		= ACCGR_RADCON_15
		CDB_TAProduct::SizeID = DN_15
	}
}

						{
							0													// isDeleted
							1                                                   // isAvailable
							0                                                   // isHidden
							1                                                   // isFix
							0                                                   // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
							0                                                   // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
							0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
						}
						0.6e+6 \ 1.0e+6                 					// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
						NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
						120.0                                               // Tmax in �C
						-10.0                                               // Tmin in �C
					}
					"3711-01.000"                       				// Reference to the TA Product
					"V-exact II 10(3/8")"                               // Name of the product
					TRVTYPE_PRESET                                      // Identifier of the valve type
					FAM_VEXACT2                                         // Identifier of the family of the product
					VERS_ANGLE                                          // Identifier of the version of the product
					1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
					""                                                  // Product comment
					"TA_TRV"                                            // Product image ID
					NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the accessory group
					#ePartOfaSetNo                                      // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
					NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
					0.0                                                 // Price of the product
					#eProduct                              	            // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
					NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
					0                                                   // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
					NO_ID                                      	        // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
					NO_ID										        // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth
				}
				BDY_GUNMETALNIKPLT                      			// Identifier of the body material
				DN_10                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
				CONN_RADUN_THR                                      // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
				""                                                  // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
				0                                                   // CBI compatibility Index
				""                                                  // CBI Version
				3.0e+4                                              // Maximum Dp of the valve
				#eMeasPointNone                                     // Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
				#eMeasDataNone                                      // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the inlet size ID
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the outlet size ID
			}
			NO_ID                                       		// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in ThermoCharID
		}
		0.86                                            	// Kvs of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Stroke of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Rangeability of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
		ACTGR_HEIM_TRV                                      // Identifier of the actuator group
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the CV adapter group
		CP_TRV                                              // Identifier of the control properties
		#eCVAdapterListNA                               	// Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                            // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
	}
	C_VEXACT2                                           // Identifier of the thermostatic characteristic
	""													// Description of the product
}

					"3652-01.000"  										// Reference to the TA Product
					"Calypso F-exact 10"                                // Name of the product
					TRVTYPE_PRESET                                      // Identifier of the valve type
					FAM_CALYFEXACT                                      // Identifier of the family of the product
					VERS_STRAIGHT                                       // Identifier of the version of the product
					1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
					""                                                  // Product comment
					"TA_TRV"                                            // Product image ID
					NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the accessory group
					#ePartOfaSetNo                                      // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
					NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
					0.0                                                 // Price of the product
					#eProduct                              	            // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
					NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
					0                                                   // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
					NO_ID                                      	        // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
					NO_ID										        // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth
				}
				BDY_BRASS 											// Identifier of the body material
				DN_10                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
				CONN_RADUN_THR                                      // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
				""                                                  // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
				0                                                   // CBI compatibility Index
				""                                                  // CBI Version
				2.0e+4                                              // Maximum Dp of the valve
				#eMeasPointNone                                     // Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
				#eMeasDataNone                                      // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
				NO_ID											// Identifier of the inlet size ID
				NO_ID											// Identifier of the outlet size ID
			}
			NO_ID                                    			// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in ThermoCharID
		}
		0.544												// Kvs of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Stroke of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Rangeability of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
		ACTGR_HEIM_TRV                                      // Identifier of the actuator group
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the CV adapter group
		CP_TRV                                              // Identifier of the control properties
		#eCVAdapterListNA									// Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                            // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
	}
	C_CALYPSOTRV3											// Identifier of the thermostatic characteristic
	""					                                    // Description of the product
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		CDB_FlowLimitedControlValve : This is a control valve for radiator that has a flow limited built-in.
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	new:CDB_FlowLimitedControlValve(ID)->tableID	Common CData syntax
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						{
//							{
//								0				isDeleted
//								1				isAvailable
//								0				isHidden
//								1				isFix
//								0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//								0				Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
//      						0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//							}
//							Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//							PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//							Tmax in �C
//							Tmin in �C
//						}
//						"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//						"Name"					Name of the product
//						TypeID					Identifier of the valve type
//						FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//						VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//						PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//						Comment					Product comment
//						ProdImgID				Product image ID
//						AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//						PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
//						TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//						Price					Price of the product
// 						ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//						AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//						isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   					AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//						AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//					}
//					BodyMaterialID			Identifier of the body material
//					SizeID					Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//					ConnectID				Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//					ConnTabID				Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//					Conn2ID					Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//					CBIType					Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//					CBISize					Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//					CBISizeInch				Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//					CBICompatibilityIndex	CBI compatibility Index
//					CBIVersion				CBI Version
//					Dpmax					Maximum Dp of the valve
//					MeasPt					Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
//					MeasurableData			Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
//					InletSizeID				Identifier of the inlet size ID
//					OutletSizeID			Identifier of the outlet size ID
//				}
//				CharactID			// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in FLCVCharID
//			}
//			Kvs					Kvs of the CV
//			Stroke				Stroke of the CV
//			Rangeability		Rangeability of the CV
//			LeakageRate			Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
//			CloseOffCharID		Identifier of the close-off characteristic
//			ActuatorGroupID		Identifier of the actuator group
//			CvAdapterGroupID	Identifier of the CV adapter group
//			CtrlPropID			Identifier of the control properties
//		}
//		FLCVCharID			Identifier of the flow limited control valve characteristic
//		"Description"		Description of the product
//	}
//
// Inherited files
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_TAProduct::BodyMaterialID
//	CDB_TAProduct::SizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnectID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnTabID
//	CDB_TAProduct::Conn2ID
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIType
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISize
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISizeInch
//  CDB_TAProduct::CBICompatibilityIndex
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIVersion
//	CDB_TAProduct::Dpmax
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasPt
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasurableData
//	CDB_TAProduct::InletSizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::OutletSizeID
//	CDB_RegulatingValve::CharactID
//	CDB_ControlValve::Kvs
//	CDB_ControlValve::Stroke
//	CDB_ControlValve::Rangeability
//	CDB_ControlValve::LeakageRate
//	CDB_ControlValve::CloseOffCharID
//	CDB_ControlValve::ActuatorGroupID
//	CDB_ControlValve::CvAdapterGroupID
//	CDB_ControlValve::CtrlPropID
//	CDB_ControlValve::AdapterListMode
//	CDB_FlowLimitedControlValve::FLCVCharID
//	CDB_FlowLimitedControlValve::Description

					FAM_ECLIPSEZ                                        // Identifier of the family of the product
					VERS_STRAIGHT                                       // Identifier of the version of the product
					1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
					""                                                  // Product comment
					"TA_TRV"                                            // Product image ID
					ACCGR_RADCON_10                                     // Identifier of the accessory group
					#ePartOfaSetNo                                      // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
					NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
					0.0                                                 // Price of the product
					#eProduct                       					// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
					NO_ID                           					// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
					0                               					// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
					NO_ID                           					// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
					NO_ID												// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
				}
				BDY_BRASSLEADFREE                          			// Identifier of the body material
				DN_10                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
				CONN_RADUN_THR                                      // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
				""                                                  // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
				0                                                   // CBI compatibility Index
				""                                                  // CBI Version
				6.0e+4                                              // Maximum Dp of the valve
				#eMeasPointNone                                     // Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
				#eMeasDataNone                                      // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the inlet size ID
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the outlet size ID
			}
			NO_ID                                           	// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in FLCVCharID
		}
		0.0                                                 // Kvs of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Stroke of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Rangeability of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
		ACTGR_HEIM_FLC                                      // Identifier of the actuator group
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the CV adapter group
		CP_RVT                                              // Identifier of the control properties
		#eCVAdapterListNA                                   // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
	                                                        // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
	}
	C_AEXACT                                            // Identifier of the flow limited control valve characteristic
	""		                                            // Description of the product
}

							1                                                   // isAvailable

							0                                                   // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
							0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
						}
						0.6e+6 \ 1.0e+6                 					// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
						NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
						120.0                                               // Tmax in �C
						2                                               	// Tmin in �C
					}
					"4324-03.301"                       				// Reference to the TA Product
					"IDS_THM_HEIMINSERT_VHV"                            // Name of the product
					TRVTYPE_INSERT_PRESET                               // Identifier of the valve type
					FAM_VHV                                             // Identifier of the family of the product

					1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
					""                                                  // Product comment
					"TA_TRV"                                            // Product image ID

					NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
					0.0                                                 // Price of the product

					NO_ID                           					// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)

					NO_ID												// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
				}
				BDY_BRASS                            				// Identifier of the body material
				DN_15                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
				CONN_THREADM_G12                                    // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
				""                                                  // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
				""                                                  // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II

				0                                                   // CBI compatibility Index
				""                                                  // CBI Version

				#eMeasDataNone                                      // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the inlet size ID

		}
		0.98                                            	// Kvs of the CV
		0.0                                                 // Stroke of the CV

new:CDB_RegulatingValve(RGLX_10A_RV) -> REGVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					0											// isDeleted
					1                                           // isAvailable
					0                                           // isHidden
					1                                           // isFix
					0                                           // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
					0                                           // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               							// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				0.6e+6 \ 1.0e+6         					// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                       // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				120.0                                       // Tmax in �C
				-10.0                                       // Tmin in �C
			}
			"0351-01.000"               				// Reference to the TA Product
			"Regulux 10 (3/8")"                         // Name of the product
			RVTYPE_RV                                   // Identifier of the valve type
			FAM_REGULUX                                 // Identifier of the family of the product
			VERS_ANGLE                                  // Identifier of the version of the product
			1                                           // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			""                                          // Product comment
			"TA_DRV_S"                                  // Product image ID
			NO_ID                                       // Identifier of the accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                              // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID										// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                         // Price of the product
			#eProduct                       			// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                               			// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
			NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
			NO_ID										// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
		}
		BDY_GUNMETALNIKPLT              			// Identifier of the body material
		DN_10                                       // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
		CONN_RADUN_THR                              // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
		NO_ID                                       // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
		NO_ID                                       // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
		""                                          // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
		""                                          // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
		""                                          // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
		0                                           // CBI compatibility Index
		""                                          // CBI Version
		0.0                                         // Maximum Dp of the valve
		#eMeasPointNone                             // Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
		#eMeasDataNone                              // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
		NO_ID										// Identifier of the inlet size ID
		NO_ID										// Identifier of the outlet size ID	
	}
	C_REGULUX                           		// Identifier of the regulating valve characteristic.
}

//
//		Table ACTUATOR_TAB : Actuators

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	new:CDB_ThermostaticActuator(ID)->ACTUATOR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						0				isDeleted
//						1				isAvailable
//						0				isHidden
//						1				isFix
//						0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
//						0				Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc). (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//      				0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//					}
//					Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//					PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//					Tmax in �C
//					Tmin in �C
//				}
//				"Reference"				Reference to the product.
//				"Name"					Name of the product
//				TypeID					Identifier of the valve type 
//				FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//				VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//				PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//				Comment					Product comment
//				ProdImgID				Product image ID
//				AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//				PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//				TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//				Price					Price of the product
//				Price					Price of the product
// 				ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//				AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//				isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   			AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//				AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//			}
//			OpeningType			Opening type (Linear or Circular)
//			MaxForceTorque		Max force or torque developped by the actuator
//			MinLimitedStroke	Min. limited stroke of the actuator
//			MaxStroke			Max stroke of the actuator (in m for #eOPENTYPE_Linear; in � for #eOPENTYPE_Circ)
//			ActAdapterGroupID	Identifier of the actuator adapter group
//			MinEnvTemp			Min temperature for operating environment in �C
//			MaxEnvTemp			Max temperature for operating environment in �C
//		}
//		MinSetting			Min setting temperature (�C)
//		MaxSetting			Max setting temperature (�C)
//		CapillaryLength		Length of the capillary tube if exist
//		Hysteresis			Hysteresis in K
//		FrostProtection		Frost protection temperature (�C)
//	}
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_Actuator::OpeningType
//	CDB_Actuator::MaxForceTorque
//	CDB_Actuator::MinLimitedStroke
//	CDB_Actuator::LimitedStrokeMode
//	CDB_Actuator::MaxStroke
//	CDB_Actuator::ActAdapterGroupID
//  CDB_Actuator::MinEnvTemp
//  CDB_Actuator::MaxEnvTemp
//	CDB_ThermostaticActuator::MinSetting
//	CDB_ThermostaticActuator::MaxSetting

//	CDB_ThermostaticActuator::Hysteresis
//	CDB_ThermostaticActuator::FrostProtection

new:CDB_ThermostaticActuator(ACT_K_HEAD_BI_A) -> ACTUATOR_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					0                   					// isDeleted
					1                               		// isAvailable
					0                               		// isHidden
					1                               		// isFix
					0                               		// Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
					0                               		// Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               						// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				0 \ DBL_MAX								// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                   // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				100                                     // Tmax in �C: Max media temperature in �C
				0                                       // Tmin in �C: Min media temperature in �C
			}
			"6000-00.500"              				// Reference to the TA Product
			"IDS_K_HEAD"                    		// Name of the product
			ACTTYP_THRMBUILTIN                      // Identifier of the actuator type
			ACTFAM_K_HEAD_BUILTIN                   // Identifier of the family of the product
			ACTVER_STD                              // Identifier of the actuator version
			1										// Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			"IDS_K_HEAD_BI_A_DESC"                  // Description of the product
			"NO_ID"									// Product image ID
			ACCGR_DDXKHEAD                          // Identifier of the actuator accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                          // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID									// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                     // Price of the product
			#eProduct                       		// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                           		// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                               		// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
			NO_ID                           		// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
			NO_ID									// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
		}
		#eOPENTYPE_Linear               		// Opening type (Linear or Circular)
		-1                              		// Max force or torque developped by the actuator
		-1                              		// Min. limited stroke of the actuator
		#eLimitedStrokeMode_Electronic			// Limited stroke mode of the actuator
		-1                              		// Max stroke of the actuator (in m for #eOPENTYPE_Linear; in � for #eOPENTYPE_Circ)
		NO_ID						    		// Identifier of the actuator adapter group
		DBL_MIN									// Min temperature for operating environment in �C
		50										// Max temperature for operating environment in �C
	}
	6     							// Min setting temperature (�C)
	28                              // Max setting temperature (�C)
	-1                              // Length of the capillary tube if exist
	0.2                             // Hysteresis in K
	6                               // Frost protection temperature (�C)
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table TRVHEADSET_TAB : Thermostatic valve/Head sets
// When reading CDB_Set object (txt file) TAS4 will update
// First and Second ID, TA_Product::PartOfASet member variable
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	new:CDB_Set(ID)->TRVHEADSET_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			0				isDeleted
//			1				isAvailable
//			0				isHidden
//			1				isFix
//			0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
//			0				Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
//      	0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//		}
//		"Reference"			Reference to the TA Product
//		"Name"				Name of the product
//		FirstID				Identifier of the control valve
//		SecondID			Identifier of the actuator
//		AccessGroupID		Identifier of the accessory group
//		"Parameter"			String to allow to apply some filter.
//  	"NextID"			Identifier of the next ID to consider can be Set ID, Group ID, Product ID etc...
//	}
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_Set::Reference
//	CDB_Set::Name
//	CDB_Set::FirstID
//	CDB_Set::SecondID
//	CDB_Set::AccGroupID
//	CDB_Set::Parameter
//	CDB_Set::NextID
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

	{
		0														// isDeleted

		1                                           		    // isFix
		0                                           		    // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
		0                                           		    // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
		0               										// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
	}
	"3500-12.800"                       					// Reference to the TA Product
	"Retrofit insert DN 15 + Head K"                		// Name of the product
	THM_HEIMINSERT_RETRO_SA                         		// Identifier of the control valve

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table FLOORHCONTROL_TAB : Floor heating manifold products
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	How to write a floor heating manifold information ?
//	-----------------------------------------------
//
//	new:CDB_FloorHeatingManifold(ID)->FLOORHCONTROL_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					0				isDeleted
//					1				isAvailable
//					0				isHidden
//					1				isFix
//					0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//					0				Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//					0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//				}
//				Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//				PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//				Tmax in �C
//				Tmin in �C
//			}
//			"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//			"Name"					Name of the product
//			TypeID					Identifier of the valve type 
//			FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//			VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//			PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//			Comment					Product comment
//			ProdImgID				Product image ID
//			AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//			PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//			Price					Price of the product
//		}
//		HeatingCircuits			Define the number of heating circuits.
//	}
//
// Inherited files
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_FloorHeatingManifold::HeatingCircuits
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

/////////////////////////////////
// *** Dynacon 150 ****
/////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_FloorHeatingManifold(DYNACON150_2) -> FLOORHCONTROL_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				0						// isDeleted
				1                       // isAvailable
				0                       // isHidden
				1                       // isFix
				0                       // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
				101                     // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               		// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			0.6e+6 \ 6.0e+5   		// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID                   // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			70.0                    // Tmax in �C
			2.0                     // Tmin in �C
		}
		"9346-02.800"  			// Reference to the TA Product
		"Dynacon 150"       	// Name of the product
		FHCTYPE_MANIFOLD        // Identifier of the valve type
		FAM_DYNACON150          // Identifier of the family of the product
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the version of the product
		1                       // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		""                      // Product comment
		"NO_ID"                 // Product image ID
		ACCGR_DYNACON150    	// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo          // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
		NO_ID					// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0                     // Price of the product
		#eProduct               // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                       // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID					// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth
	}
	2                       // Define the number of heating circuits.
}

new:CDB_FloorHeatingManifold(DYNACON150_3) -> FLOORHCONTROL_TAB
{ Inherited(DYNACON150_2)
	{
		CDB_Product::Reference	=	"9346-03.800"
		CDB_FloorHeatingManifold::HeatingCircuits = 3
	}

new:CDB_FloorHeatingManifold(DYNALUX_3) -> FLOORHCONTROL_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				0						// isDeleted
				1                       // isAvailable
				0                       // isHidden
				1                       // isFix
				0                       // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
				101                     // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               		// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			0.6e+6 \ 6.0e+5   		// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID                   // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			60.0                    // Tmax in �C
			-5.0                    // Tmin in �C
		}
		"9320-03.800"  			// Reference to the TA Product
		"Dynalux"       		// Name of the product
		FHCTYPE_MANIFOLD        // Identifier of the valve type
		FAM_DYNALUX          	// Identifier of the family of the product
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the version of the product
		1                       // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		""                      // Product comment
		"NO_ID"                 // Product image ID
		ACCGR_DYNALUX    		// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo          // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
		NO_ID					// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0                     // Price of the product
		#eProduct               // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                       // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID					// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth
	}
	3                       // Define the number of heating circuits.
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	How to write a floor heating control valve information ?
//	-----------------------------------------------
//
//	new:CDB_FloorHeatingValve(ID)->FLOORHCONTROL_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					0							isDeleted
//					1							isAvailable
//					0							isHidden
//					1							isFix
//					0							Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//					0							Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//					0               			Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//				}
//				Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax 		in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//				PNRangeID					Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//				Tmax in �C
//				Tmin in �C
//			}
//			"Reference"					Reference to the TA Product
//			"Name"						Name of the product
//			TypeID						Identifier of the valve type 
//			FamilyID					Identifier of the family of the product
//			VersionID					Identifier of the version of the product
//			PriorityLevel				Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//			Comment						Product comment
//			ProdImgID					Product image ID
//			AccessGroupID				Identifier of the accessory group
//			PartOfaSet					Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//			Price						Price of the product
//		}
//		SupplyOrLockshield			0 = Supply, 1 = Lockshield
//		ConnectInletTypeID			Connection inlet type ID.
//		ConnectInletSizeID			Connection inlet size ID.
// 		ConnectOutletTypeID			Connection outlet type ID.
// 		ConnectOutletSizeID			Connection outlet size ID.
//		Handwheel					0 = without handweel, 1 = with handwheel.
//	}
//
// Inherited files
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_FloorHeatingValve::SupplyOrLockshield
//	CDB_FloorHeatingValve::ConnectInletTypeID
//	CDB_FloorHeatingValve::ConnectInletSizeID
//	CDB_FloorHeatingValve::ConnectOutletTypeID
//	CDB_FloorHeatingValve::ConnectOutletSizeID
//	CDB_FloorHeatingValve::Handwheel
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

/////////////////////////////////
// *** Supply pipe control valve ****
/////////////////////////////////

// Straight DN 15 (1/2�) - Connection Rp 1/2 sleeve female thread - with handwheel
new:CDB_FloorHeatingValve(FLOORHEATVALVE_SUPA) -> FLOORHCONTROL_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				0										// isDeleted
				1                       				// isAvailable
				0                       				// isHidden
				1                       				// isFix
				0                       				// Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
				101                       				// Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               						// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			0.6e+6 \ 1.0e+6   						// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID                   				// PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			120.0                   				// Tmax in �C
			-10.0                   				// Tmin in �C
		}
		"1302-02.000"  							// Reference to the TA Product
		"IDS_FLOORHEATINGVALVE_SUPPLY"     		// Name of the product
		FHCTYPE_MANIFOLD        				// Identifier of the valve type
		FAM_CTRLVALVEFH        					// Identifier of the family of the product
		NO_ID                   				// Identifier of the version of the product
		1                       				// Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		"IDS_FLOORHEATINGVALVE_DESC"     		// Product comment
		"NO_ID"                 				// Product image ID
		ACCGR_CTRLVALVEH    					// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo          				// Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
		NO_ID									// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0                     				// Price of the product
		#eProduct               				// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                   				// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                       				// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                   				// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID									// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth
	}
	0										// 0 = without handweel, 1 = with handwheel.
	CONN_THR_F_RP                   		// Connection inlet type ID.
	CONSIZE_FRP1_2                   		// Connection inlet size ID.	
	CONN_THREADM							// Connection outlet type ID.
	CONSIZE_MG3_4							// Connection outlet type ID.	
	1										// 0 = without handweel, 1 = with handwheel.
}

// Straight DN 15 (1/2�) - Connection Rp 1/2 sleeve female thread - without handwheel
new:CDB_FloorHeatingValve(FLOORHEATVALVE_SUPB) -> FLOORHCONTROL_TAB
{ Inherited(FLOORHEATVALVE_SUPA)
	{
		CDB_Product::Reference	=	"1322-02.000"
		CDB_FloorHeatingValve::Handwheel = 0
	}
}

		CDB_FloorHeatingValve::ConnectInletSizeID = CONSIZE_MR1_2
	}
}

	}

{
	{
		{
			{
				0						// isDeleted
				1                       // isAvailable
				0                       // isHidden
				1                       // isFix
				0                       // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
				101                     // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               		// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			0.6e+6 \ 1.0e+6   		// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID                   // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			90.0                    // Tmax in �C
			2.0                     // Tmin in �C
		}
		"9302-00.800"  			// Reference to the TA Product
		"Multibox K"    		// Name of the product
		FHCTYPE_CONTROLLER      // Identifier of the valve type
		FAM_MULTIBOX       		// Identifier of the family of the product
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the version of the product
		1                       // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		""                      // Product comment
		"NO_ID"                 // Product image ID
		ACCGR_MULTIBOX 			// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo          // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
		NO_ID					// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0                     // Price of the product
		#eProduct               // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                       // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                   // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID					// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth
	}
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table TAPCONTROL_TAB : Tap water control products
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	How to write a tap water control information ?
//	-----------------------------------------------
//
//	new:CDB_TapWaterControl(ID)->BALCTRLVALV_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						{
//							{
//								0				isDeleted
//								1				isAvailable
//								0				isHidden
//								1				isFix
//								0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//								0				Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//								0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//							}
//							Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//							PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//							Tmax in �C
//							Tmin in �C
//						}
//					"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//					"Name"					Name of the product
//					TypeID					Identifier of the valve type 
//					FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//					VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//					PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//					Comment					Product comment
//					ProdImgID				Product image ID
//					AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//					PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//					Price					Price of the product
//				}
//				BodyMaterialID			Identifier of the body material
//				SizeID					Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//				ConnectID				Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//				ConnTabID				Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//				Conn2ID					Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//				CBIType					Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//				CBISize					Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//				CBISizeInch				Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//				CBICompatibilityIndex	CBI compatibility Index
//				CBIVersion				CBI Version
//				Dpmax					Maximum Dp of the valve
//				MeasPt					Measuring points
//				MeasurableData			Measurable data
//				InletSizeID				Identifier of the inlet size ID
//				OutletSizeID			Identifier of the outlet size ID
//			}
//			CharactID				Identifier of the valve characteristic
//		}
//		MinTemp					Min. temperature of the adjustable range.
//		MaxTemp					Max. temperature of the adjustable range.
//      HotWaterMainsSizeID		Identifier of the hot water mains input size ID.
//	}
//
// Inherited files
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_TAProduct::BodyMaterialID
//	CDB_TAProduct::SizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnectID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnTabID
//	CDB_TAProduct::Conn2ID
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIType
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISize
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISizeInch
//  CDB_TAProduct::CBICompatibilityIndex
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIVersion
//	CDB_TAProduct::Dpmax
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasPt
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasurableData
//	CDB_TAProduct::InletSizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::OutletSizeID
//	CDB_RegulatingValve::CharactID
//	CDB_TapWaterControl::MinTemp
//	CDB_TapWaterControl::MaxTemp
//	CDB_TapWaterControl::HotWaterMainsSizeID
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


//****************************
// Mixing valves

/////////////////////////////////
// *** TA-MATIC ****
/////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_TapWaterControl(TAMATIC_20) -> TAPCONTROL_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					{
						0													// isDeleted
						1                                                   // isAvailable
						0                                                   // isHidden
						1                                                   // isFix
						0                                                   // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
						101                                                 // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
						0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
					}
					0.6e+6 \ 1.0e+6   									// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
					NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
					90.0                                               	// Tmax in �C
					0.0                                               	// Tmin in �C
				}
				"344010-20506"  									// Reference to the TA Product
				"TA-MATIC DN20"                                		// Name of the product
				TAPCTRLTYPE_MIX                                     // Identifier of the valve type
				FAM_TAMATIC                                         // Identifier of the family of the product
				NO_ID                                       		// Identifier of the version of the product
				1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
				""                                                  // Product comment
				"NO_ID"                                            	// Product image ID
				ACCGR_TAMATICDN20A                                  // Identifier of the accessory group
				#ePartOfaSetNo                                      // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
				NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
				0.0                                                 // Price of the product
				#eProduct                              	            // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
				0                                                   // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
				NO_ID                                      	        // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
				NO_ID										        // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth
			}
			BDY_GUNMETAL										// Identifier of the body material
			DN_20                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
			CONN_THREADM                                      	// Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
